Chatterji (tabla)– Mode Mâlkosh Pour Flute (The Mode Malkosh played on the flute with Tabla) | Narayan Das Mishra (sarangi) &amp; Mishra Shyam Lal (tabla) – Mode Todi Pour Sarangi (The Mode Todi played on the Sarangi) | Swami D.R. Parvatikar– Gat Pour Vinâ (Gat in the mode Kamavardhani) | Chatur Lal– Tabla Solo | Ravi Shankar (sitar), Ali Akbar Khan (sarod) &amp; Chaturial (tabla) – Sitar , Sarode Et Tablâ Mode Mauj-Khammaj, rhythm Tritâla | Mohin Ud Din Dagar &amp; Amin Ud Din Dagar (aka the Dagar Brothers) – Alâpa in the mode Multâni | Ali Akbar Khan (sarod)– Le Mode Sindhi-Bhairavi (The Mode Sindhi-bhairavi) | Raghunath Prasanna &amp; Motilal (Khurdak drums) – Thumri Pour Flute (Thumri in the mode Tilang, on the flute) | Swami D.R. Parvatikar– Svara Mandala, mode Brindâvani-tilang (The mode Brindâvani-tilang on the Svara-mandala) | Nandan Prasad (vocals) &amp; Shyam Lal (tabla)– Bhajana de Mirâ Bai (The Hindi Bhajan of Mira Bai, in the mode Mâlkosh) | Swami D.R. Parvatikar– Mode Suha-kamode Pour Vina (The Mode Suha-kamod played on the Vinâ) | Bala Sarasvati Orchestra– Jatisvaram | P.R. Balasubramanyam– Alapana, Mode Todi du Sud (Alapana in the Southern Todi mode) | K.S. Pichiappa of Tanjore (1st Nâgasvaram), K.M. Dakshinamurti (2nd Nâgasvaram), T. Subrahmanya Pillai (violin) &amp; Muthu Kumaram (percussion-thaval, jhalan(small cymbals), uttu (a nâgasvaram giving the tonic)– Alapana dans le mode Kambodhi, Pour Nagasvaram (Alapana in the mode Kambodhi) | Mrs. Kamala Krishnamurti– Kriti (in Telugu with an Alâpa in the mode Yadukula-Kambodhi) | K. Ganeshan (vocals in rhythm Tisra-Eku)– Tirmana, Mode Bhairavi (presentation of a dance-rhythm in the Southern Bhairavi mode) | Damal Krishna Pattamal (vocals), Tiruvallur Subrahmanyam (violin), Palghat Kunjumani (two mrindangams) &amp; Shiva Pattamal (tanpurâ)– Mode Varali | Budalur Krishnamurti Shastri (Veena [Gottuvâdyam]) , Varahur Muthusvami Aiyar (violin) &amp; Tinniyam Venkatarama Aiyar (Mrindangam)– Ganesha Kimaram pour gottuvadyam | Mudi Kondan C. Venkatarama Iyer (vocals), Vellore Gopalachari (vocals), M. Chandrashekharan (violin) &amp; Karaikudi MuthaIyer (mrindangam) – Pallavi, Mode Bhairavi Du Sud (Pallavi in the Southern Bhairavi mode, Rhythm Triputa) | Tanjore Viswanathan (flute) &amp; T. Ranganathan (mrindangam)– Javâli, Mode Khamas Pour Flute (played on the flute, in the mode Khamas) | Unknown artist with accompaniment on mrindangam – Pallavi, Alâpana Et Vocalises, Mode Bhairavi Du Sud (Pallavi in the Southern Bhairavi mode) | D.K. Pattamal (vocals), Kalyan Krishna Bhagavatar (Veena [Vînâ]), &amp; Karaikudi Muttu Aiyar (Mridangam)– Javâli, Mode Paraj (Javali in the mode Paraj) | Kalyan Krishna Bhagavatar (Veena [Vînâ]), Devakotai Narayana Lyengar (Veena [Vînâ]) &amp; Karaikudi Muthu Aiyar (mridangam)– Sadhincene Pour Deux Vinâs (Sdhincene with an introdocutroy Alâpa in the mode Arabbi, interpreted on two Vînâs) | Radha Shri Ram Orchestra– Varnam, mode Dhanyasi (Varnam in the mode Dhanyasi and the rhythm Adi Tâla) | Mrs. S. Vidya– Varnam, mode Kambodhi, vinâ Solo (A Varnam in the mode Kambodhi, played on the vinâ) | Bala Sarasvati Orchestra (T. Visvanathan – flute, T. Ranganathan – mridangam | T. Visvanathan (flute) &amp; T. Ranganathan (mridangam)– Sandehamunu, Mode Râmapriyâ, pour Flute (of Tyâgaraja, in the mode Râmapriyâ, played on the flute) | Damal Krishna Pattamal (vocals), Tiruvallur Subrahmanyam (violin), Palghat Kunjumani (mridangam) &amp; Shiva Pattamal (mridangam)– Ninyâko (a Râga-mâlikâ of the 16th century) | Muttu kumaram– Solo de Mridangamar (in the rhythm Adi-tâla, with the accompaniment of small cymbals (tâlam) anda Nâgasvaram drone) | Radha Shri Ram Orchestra– Jhâna Vinayakané</yt-formatted-string>
